<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in">The tendering holder
will, upon request, execute and deliver any additional documents deemed by the Depositary or the Company to be necessary, appropriate
or convenient to complete the sale, assignment and transfer of the shares tendered.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in">If the space provided
in Box 1 above is inadequate, the certificate numbers and/or the number of shares should be listed on a separated signed schedule
that should be attached to this Letter of Transmittal.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in"><B>Partial Tenders
(Not Applicable to Shareholders Who Tender by Book-Entry Transfer).</B> If fewer than all the shares represented by any certificate
submitted to the Depositary are to be tendered, fill in the number of shares that are to be tendered in Box 1. In that case, if
any tendered shares are purchased, new certificate(s) for the remainder of the shares that were evidenced by the old certificate(s)
will be sent to the registered holder(s), unless otherwise provided in the appropriate box on this Letter of Transmittal, promptly
after the acceptance for payment of, and payment for, the shares tendered. All shares represented by certificates delivered to
the Depositary will be deemed to have been tendered unless otherwise indicated.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in">In participating in
the Offer, the tendering shareholder acknowledges that: (1) the Offer is established voluntarily by the Company, it is discretionary
in nature and it may be extended, modified, suspended or terminated by the Company as provided in the Offer to Purchase; (2) the
tendering shareholder is voluntarily participating in the Offer; (3) the future value of the shares is unknown and cannot be predicted
with certainty; (4) the tendering shareholder has received the Offer to Purchase and the Letter of Transmittal, as amended or supplemented;
(5) any foreign exchange obligations triggered by the tendering shareholder&rsquo;s tender of shares or the receipt of proceeds
are solely his or her responsibility; and (6) regardless of any action that the Company takes with respect to any or all income/capital
gains tax, social security or insurance tax, transfer tax or other tax-related items (&ldquo;Tax Items&rdquo;) related to the Offer
and the disposition of shares, the tendering shareholder acknowledges that the ultimate liability for all Tax Items is and remains
his or her sole responsibility. In that regard, the tendering shareholder authorizes the Company to withhold all applicable Tax
Items that the Depositary or other withholding agent is legally required to withhold. The tendering shareholder consents to the
collection, use and transfer, in electronic or other form, of the tendering shareholder&rsquo;s personal data as described in this
document by and among, as applicable, the Company, its subsidiaries, and third party administrators for the exclusive purpose of
implementing, administering and managing his or her participation in the Offer. No authority conferred or agreed to be conferred
by this Letter of Transmittal shall be affected by, and all such authority shall survive, the death or incapacity of the undersigned.
All obligations of the undersigned pursuant to this Letter of Transmittal shall be binding upon the heirs, personal and legal representatives,
administrators, trustees in bankruptcy, successors and assigns of the undersigned.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center"><B>IMPORTANT U.S. TAX INFORMATION FOR HOLDERS</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in">This is a summary only
of certain U.S. federal income tax considerations. Shareholders should consult with their own tax advisors regarding the tax consequences
with respect to their particular circumstances.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in">In order to avoid backup
withholding of U.S. federal income tax on payments pursuant to the Offer, a U.S. shareholder tendering shares must, unless an exemption
applies, provide the Depositary with such shareholder&rsquo;s correct taxpayer identification number (&ldquo;TIN&rdquo;), certify
under penalties of perjury that such TIN is correct (or that such shareholder is waiting for a TIN to be issued), and provide certain
other certifications by completing the IRS Form W-9 included in this Letter of Transmittal. If a shareholder does not provide his,
her or its correct TIN or fails to provide the required certifications, the IRS may impose certain penalties on such shareholder
and payment to such shareholder pursuant to the Offer may be subject to backup withholding at a rate currently equal to 24%. All
U.S. shareholders tendering shares pursuant to the Offer should complete and sign the IRS Form W-9 to provide the information and
certification necessary to avoid backup withholding (unless an applicable exemption exists and is proved in a manner satisfactory
to the Depositary). To the extent that a U.S. shareholder designates another U.S. person to receive payment, such other person
may be required to provide a properly completed IRS Form W-9 or a substitute form W-9.<BR STYLE="clear: both">
</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" STYLE="width: 100%; border-collapse: collapse; font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">

    <TD ROWSPAN="3" STYLE="padding-right: 20pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt">Enter your TIN in the appropriate box. The TIN provided must match the name given on line 1 to avoid backup withholding. For individuals, this is generally your social security number (SSN). However, for a resident alien, sole proprietor, or disregarded entity, see the instructions for Part I, later. For other entities, it is your employer identification number (EIN). If you do not have a number, see <I>How to get a TIN, </I>later.</FONT></TD>
    <TD COLSPAN="11" STYLE="border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; border-left: Black 1pt solid; padding-left: 5.4pt; border-right: Black 1pt solid"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 8pt"><B>Social security number</B></FONT></TD></TR>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 153.8pt 0pt 6pt"></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 153.8pt 0pt 6pt"></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0in; text-indent: 0in"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt">Under
penalties of perjury, I certify that:</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 6pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 9pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt">1.</FONT></TD><TD><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt">The
                                         number shown on this form is my correct taxpayer identification number (or I am waiting
                                         for a number to be issued to me); and</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif"></P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 9pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt">2.</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="padding-right: 9.5pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt">I
                                         am not subject to backup withholding because: (a) I am exempt from backup withholding,
                                         or (b) I have not been notified by the Internal Revenue Service (IRS) that I am subject
                                         to backup withholding as a result of a failure to report all interest or dividends, or
                                         (c) the IRS has notified me that I am no longer subject to backup withholding; and</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif"></P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 8.85pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt">3.</FONT></TD><TD><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt">I
                                         am a U.S. citizen or other U.S. person (defined below); and</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif"></P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 8.85pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt">4.</FONT></TD><TD><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt">The
                                         FATCA code(s) entered on this form (if any) indicating that I am exempt from FATCA reporting
                                         is correct.</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0in; text-indent: 0in"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><B>Certification
instructions.</B> You must cross out item 2 above if you have been notified by the IRS that you are currently subject to backup
withholding because you have failed to report all interest and dividends on your tax return. For real estate transactions, item
2 does not apply. For mortgage interest paid, acquisition or abandonment of secured property, cancellation of debt, contributions
to an individual retirement arrangement (IRA), and generally, payments other than interest and dividends, you are not required
to sign the certification, but you must provide your correct TIN. See the instructions for Part II, later.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0in; text-indent: 0in">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0in; text-indent: 0in"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0in; text-indent: 0in"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt">Purpose
of Form</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0in; text-indent: 0in"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0in; text-indent: 0in"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt">An
individual or entity (Form W-9 requester) who is required to file an information return with the IRS must obtain your correct
taxpayer identification number (TIN) which may be your social security number (SSN), individual taxpayer identification number
(ITIN), adoption taxpayer identification number (ATIN), or employer identification number (EIN), to report on an information return
the amount paid to you, or other amount reportable on an information return. Examples of information returns include, but are
not limited to, the following.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 6pt"></P>

<DIV STYLE="POSITION:RELATIVE;FLOAT:LEFT;WIDTH:48%">

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 13pt">By signing the filled-out form, you:</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 13pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0.05pt 0pt 6pt; text-indent: 8pt">1. Certify that the TIN you are
giving is correct (or you are waiting for a number to be issued),</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0.05pt 0pt 6pt; text-indent: 8pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 14pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 8.85pt">2.</TD><TD>Certify that you are not subject to backup withholding, or</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 2.1pt 0pt 6pt; text-indent: 8pt">3. Claim exemption from backup
withholding if you are a U.S. exempt payee. If applicable, you are also certifying that as a U.S. person, your allocable share
of any partnership income from a U.S. trade or business is not subject to the withholding tax on foreign partners' share of effectively
connected income, and</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 2.1pt 0pt 6pt; text-indent: 8pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 8.2pt 0pt 6pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: 8pt">4. Certify
that FATCA code(s) entered on this form (if any) indicating that you are exempt from the FATCA reporting, is correct. See <I>What
is FATCA reporting,</I> later, for further information.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 8.2pt 0pt 6pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: 8pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0.15pt 0pt 6pt"><B>Note:</B> If you are a U.S. person and a requester
gives you a form other than Form W-9 to request your TIN, you must use the requester&rsquo;s form if it is substantially similar
to this Form W-9.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0.15pt 0pt 6pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0.15pt 0pt 6pt"><B>Definition of a U.S. person.</B> For federal
tax purposes, you are considered a U.S. person if you are:</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0.15pt 0pt 6pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="width: 100%; font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 6pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 10pt">&#9679;</TD><TD>An individual who is a U.S. citizen or U.S. resident alien;</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="width: 100%; font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top; text-align: justify">
<TD STYLE="width: 6pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 10pt; text-align: left">&#9679;</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">A partnership, corporation, company, or association created
or organized in the United States or under the laws of the United States;</TD>
</TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 10.7pt 0pt 6pt; text-indent: 0in">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="width: 100%; font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 6pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 10pt">&#9679;</TD><TD>An estate (other than a foreign estate); or</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="width: 100%; font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 6pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 10pt">&#9679;</TD><TD>A domestic trust (as defined in Regulations section 301.7701-7).</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 6pt"><B>Special rules for partnerships.</B>
Partnerships that conduct a trade or business in the United States are generally required to pay a withholding tax under
section 1446 on any foreign partners&rsquo; share of effectively connected taxable income from such business. Further, in
certain cases where a Form W-9 has not been received, the rules under section 1446 require a partnership to presume that a
partner is a foreign person, and pay the section 1446 withholding tax. Therefore, if you are a U.S. person that is a partner
in a partnership conducting a trade or business in the United States, provide Form W-9 to the partnership to establish your
U.S. status and avoid section 1446 withholding on your share of partnership income.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0.15pt 0pt 6pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0.15pt 0pt 6pt; text-indent: 8pt">In the cases below, the following
person must give Form W-9 to the partnership for purposes of establishing its U.S. status and avoiding withholding on its allocable
share of net income from the partnership conducting a trade or business in the United States.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0.15pt 0pt 6pt; text-indent: 8pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="width: 100%; font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 6pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 10pt; text-align: left">&#9679;</TD><TD>In the case of a disregarded entity with a U.S. owner,
the U.S. owner of the disregarded entity and not the entity;</TD>
</TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 7.6pt 0pt 6pt; text-indent: 0in">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="width: 100%; font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 6pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 10pt; text-align: left">&#9679;</TD><TD>In the case of a grantor trust with a U.S. grantor or
other U.S. owner, generally, the U.S. grantor or other U.S. owner of the grantor trust and not the trust; and</TD>
</TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 7.6pt 0pt 6pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="width: 100%; font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 6pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 10pt; text-align: left">&#9679;</TD><TD>In the case of a U.S. trust (other than a grantor trust),
the U.S. trust (other than a grantor trust) and not the beneficiaries of the trust.</TD>
</TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 14.1pt 0pt 6pt; text-indent: 0in">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0.15pt 0pt 6pt"><B>Foreign person.</B> If you are a foreign person
or the U.S. branch of a foreign bank that has elected to be treated as a U.S. person, do not use Form W-9. Instead, use the appropriate
Form W-8 or Form 8233 (see Pub. 515, Withholding of Tax on Nonresident Aliens and Foreign Entities).</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0.15pt 0pt 6pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0.15pt 0pt 6pt"><B>Nonresident alien who becomes a resident alien.</B>
Generally, only a nonresident alien individual may use the terms of a tax treaty to reduce or eliminate U.S. tax on certain types
of income. However, most tax treaties contain a provision known as a &ldquo;saving clause.&rdquo; Exceptions specified in the saving
clause may permit an exemption from tax to continue for certain types of income even after the payee has otherwise become a U.S.
resident alien for tax purposes.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0.15pt 0pt 6pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 4.1pt 0pt 6pt; text-indent: 8pt">If you are a U.S. resident alien
who is relying on an exception contained in the saving clause of a tax treaty to claim an exemption from U.S. tax on certain types
of income, you must attach a statement to Form W-9 that specifies the following five items.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 4.1pt 0pt 6pt; text-indent: 8pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 9.6pt 0pt 6pt; text-indent: 8pt">1. The treaty country. Generally,
this must be the same treaty under which you claimed exemption from tax as a nonresident alien.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 9.6pt 0pt 6pt; text-indent: 8pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 14pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 8.85pt">2.</TD><TD>The treaty article addressing the income.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 10.95pt 0pt 6pt; text-indent: 8pt">3. The article number (or location)
in the tax treaty that contains the saving clause and its exceptions.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 10.95pt 0pt 6pt; text-indent: 8pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 14.95pt 0pt 6pt; text-indent: 8pt">4. The type and amount of income
that qualifies for the exemption from tax.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 14.95pt 0pt 6pt; text-indent: 8pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 2.8pt 0pt 6pt; text-indent: 8pt">5. Sufficient facts to justify
the exemption from tax under the terms of the treaty article.</P>

</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="POSITION:RELATIVE;FLOAT:RIGHT;WIDTH:48%">

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 7.15pt 0pt 6pt; text-indent: 7pt"><B><I>Example.</I></B>
Article 20 of the U.S.-China income tax treaty allows an exemption from tax for scholarship income received by a Chinese
student temporarily present in the United States. Under U.S. law, this student will become a resident alien for tax purposes
if his or her stay in the United States exceeds 5 calendar years. However, paragraph 2 of the first Protocol to the
U.S.-China treaty (dated April 30, 1984) allows the provisions of Article 20 to continue to apply even after the Chinese
student becomes a resident alien of the United States. A Chinese student who qualifies for this exception (under paragraph 2
of the first protocol) and is relying on this exception to claim an exemption from tax on his or her scholarship or
fellowship income would attach to Form W-9 a statement that includes the information described above to support that
exemption.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 6.3pt 0pt 6pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 6.05pt 0pt 6pt; text-indent: 8pt">If you are a nonresident alien
or a foreign entity, give the requester the appropriate completed Form W-8 or Form 8233.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 6.05pt 0pt 6pt; text-indent: 8pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 6pt">Backup Withholding</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 6pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 6.3pt 0pt 6pt"><B>What is backup withholding? </B>Persons making
certain payments to you must under certain conditions withhold and pay to the IRS 28% of such payments. This is called &ldquo;backup
withholding.&rdquo; Payments that may be subject to backup withholding include interest, tax-exempt interest, dividends, broker
and barter exchange transactions, rents, royalties, nonemployee pay, payments made in settlement of payment card and third party
network transactions, and certain payments from fishing boat operators. Real estate transactions are not subject to backup withholding.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 6.3pt 0pt 6pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 9.5pt 0pt 6pt; text-indent: 7pt">You will not be subject to backup
withholding on payments you receive if you give the requester your correct TIN, make the proper certifications, and report all
your taxable interest and dividends on your tax return.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 9.5pt 0pt 6pt; text-indent: 7pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 6pt"><B>Payments you receive will be subject to backup withholding
if:</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 6pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 1.6pt 0pt 6pt; text-indent: 8pt">1. You do not furnish your TIN
to the requester,</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 1.6pt 0pt 6pt; text-indent: 8pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 12.6pt 0pt 6pt; text-indent: 8pt">2. You do not certify your TIN
when required (see the instructions for Part II for details),</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 12.6pt 0pt 6pt; text-indent: 8pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 14pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 8.85pt">3.</TD><TD>The IRS tells the requester that you furnished an incorrect TIN,</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 16.85pt 0pt 6pt; text-indent: 8pt">4. The IRS tells you that you
are subject to backup withholding because you did not report all your interest and dividends on your tax return (for reportable
interest and dividends only), or</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 16.85pt 0pt 6pt; text-indent: 8pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 11.35pt 0pt 6pt; text-indent: 8pt">5. You do not certify to the
requester that you are not subject to backup withholding under 4 above (for reportable interest and dividend accounts opened after
1983 only).</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 11.35pt 0pt 6pt; text-indent: 8pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 6.3pt 0pt 6pt; text-indent: 8pt">Certain payees and payments are
exempt from backup withholding. See <I>Exempt payee code,</I> later, and the separate Instructions for the Requester of Form W-9
for more information.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 6.3pt 0pt 6pt; text-indent: 8pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 13pt">Also see <I>Special rules for partnerships,</I> earlier.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 13pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 6pt">What is FATCA Reporting?</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 6pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 11.35pt 0pt 6pt">The Foreign Account Tax Compliance Act (FATCA)
requires a participating foreign financial institution to report all United States account holders that are specified United States
persons. Certain payees are exempt from FATCA reporting. See <I>Exemption from FATCA reporting code,</I> later, and the Instructions
for the Requester of Form W-9 for more information.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 6pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 6pt">Updating Your Information</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 6pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 6.05pt 0pt 6pt">You must provide updated information to any person
to whom you claimed to be an exempt payee if you are no longer an exempt payee and anticipate receiving reportable payments in
the future from this person. For example, you may need to provide updated information if you are a C corporation that elects to
be an S corporation, or if you no longer are tax exempt. In addition, you must furnish a new Form W-9 if the name or TIN changes
for the account; for example, if the grantor of a grantor trust dies.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 6.05pt 0pt 6pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 6pt">Penalties</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 6pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 9.5pt 0pt 6pt"><B>Failure to furnish TIN.</B> If you fail to furnish
your correct TIN to a requester, you are subject to a penalty of $50 for each such failure unless your failure is due to reasonable
cause and not to willful neglect.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 9.5pt 0pt 6pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 9.5pt 0pt 6pt"><B>Civil penalty for false information with respect
to withholding.</B> If you make a false statement with no reasonable basis that results in no backup withholding, you are subject
to a $500 penalty.</P>
</DIV>
<BR CLEAR="ALL"><BR>
<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 9.5pt 0pt 6pt">&nbsp;</P>

    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 12pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid"><P STYLE="margin-top: 0pt; text-align: center; margin-bottom: 0pt; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><!-- Field: Sequence; Type: Arabic; Name: PageNo -->7<!-- Field: /Sequence --></P></DIV>
    <DIV STYLE="page-break-before: always; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 6pt"><P STYLE="margin: 0pt">&nbsp;</P></DIV>
    <!-- Field: /Page -->

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0.2pt 0pt 6pt">&nbsp;</P>
<!-- Field: Rule-Page --><DIV ALIGN="LEFT" STYLE="margin-top: 3pt; margin-bottom: 8pt"><DIV STYLE="font-size: 1pt; border-top: Black 1pt solid; width: 100%">&nbsp;</DIV></DIV><!-- Field: /Rule-Page -->
<DIV STYLE="POSITION:RELATIVE;FLOAT:LEFT;WIDTH:48%">
<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0.2pt 0pt 6pt"><B>Criminal penalty for falsifying information.</B>
Willfully falsifying certifications or affirmations may subject you to criminal penalties including fines and/or imprisonment.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0.2pt 0pt 6pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 6pt"><B>Misuse of TINs.</B> If the requester discloses or
uses TINs in violation of federal law, the requester may be subject to civil and criminal penalties.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 6pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 6pt">Specific Instructions</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 6pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 6pt">Line 1</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 6pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 6pt">You must enter one of the following on this line; <B>do
not</B> leave this line blank. The name should match the name on your tax return.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 6pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0.25pt 0pt 6pt; text-indent: 8pt">If this Form W-9 is for a joint
account (other than an account maintained by a foreign financial institution (FFI)), list first, and then circle, the name of the
person or entity whose number you entered in Part I of Form W-9. If you are providing Form W-9 to an FFI to document a joint account,
each holder of the account that is a U.S. person must provide a Form W-9.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0.25pt 0pt 6pt; text-indent: 8pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 3.4pt 0pt 6pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: 8pt">a.<FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;
</FONT><B>Individual.</B> Generally, enter the name shown on your tax return. If you have changed your last name without informing
the Social Security Administration (SSA) of the name change, enter your first name, the last name as shown on your social security
card, and your new last name.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 3.4pt 0pt 6pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: 8pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0.2pt 0pt 6pt"><B>Note: ITIN applicant: </B>Enter your individual
name as it was entered on your Form W-7 application, line 1a. This should also be the same as the name you entered on the Form
1040/1040A/1040EZ you filed with your application.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0.2pt 0pt 6pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 8.85pt 0pt 6pt; text-indent: 8pt">b.<FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;
</FONT><B>Sole proprietor or single-member LLC. </B>Enter your individual name as shown on your 1040/1040A/1040EZ on line 1. You
may enter your business, trade, or &ldquo;doing business as&rdquo; (DBA) name on line 2.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 8.85pt 0pt 6pt; text-indent: 8pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 6pt; text-indent: 8pt">c.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <B>Partnership, LLC
that is not a single-member LLC, C corporation, or S corporation.</B> Enter the entity's name as shown on the entity's tax return
on line 1 and any business, trade, or DBA name on line 2.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 6pt; text-indent: 8pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0.2pt 0pt 6pt; text-indent: 8pt">d.<FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;
</FONT><B>Other entities.</B> Enter your name as shown on required U.S. federal tax documents on line 1. This name should match
the name shown on the charter or other legal document creating the entity. You may enter any business, trade, or DBA name on line
2.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0.2pt 0pt 6pt; text-indent: 8pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 1.25pt 0pt 6pt; text-indent: 8pt">e.<FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;
</FONT><B>Disregarded entity.</B> For U.S. federal tax purposes, an entity that is disregarded as an entity separate from its owner
is treated as a &ldquo;disregarded entity.&rdquo; See Regulations section 301.7701-2(c)(2)(iii). Enter the owner's name on line
1. The name of the entity entered on line 1 should never be a disregarded entity. The name on line 1 should be the name shown on
the income tax return on which the income should be reported. For example, if a foreign LLC that is treated as a disregarded entity
for U.S. federal tax purposes has a single owner that is a U.S. person, the U.S. owner's name is required to be provided on line
1. If the direct owner of the entity is also a disregarded entity, enter the first owner that is not disregarded for federal tax
purposes. Enter the disregarded entity's name on line 2, &ldquo;Business name/disregarded entity name.&rdquo; If the owner of the
disregarded entity is a foreign person, the owner must complete an appropriate Form W-8 instead of a Form W-9. This is the case
even if the foreign person has a U.S. TIN.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 1.25pt 0pt 6pt; text-indent: 8pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 6pt">Line 2</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 6pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0.2pt 0pt 6pt">If you have a business name, trade name, DBA name,
or disregarded entity name, you may enter it on line 2.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0.2pt 0pt 6pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 6pt">Line 3</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 6pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 1.05pt 0pt 6pt">Check the appropriate box on line 3 for the U.S.
federal tax classification of the person whose name is entered on line 1. Check only one box on line 3.</P>

</DIV>
<DIV STYLE="POSITION:RELATIVE;FLOAT:RIGHT;WIDTH:48%"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 8pt"></FONT><TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" ALIGN="CENTER" STYLE="width: 99%; font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; border-collapse: collapse">
<TR STYLE="vertical-align: top"><TD STYLE="width: 50%; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 8pt">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="width: 50%; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 8pt">&nbsp;</FONT></TD></TR>
<TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
    <TD STYLE="border-right: black 1pt solid; border-bottom: black 1pt solid; border-left: black 1pt solid; padding-top: 1pt; padding-right: 8.05pt; padding-left: 3.7pt"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 8pt"><B>IF
    the entity/person on line 1 is a(n) . . .</B></FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="border-right: black 1pt solid; border-bottom: black 1pt solid; padding-top: 0.7pt; padding-left: 3.7pt"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 8pt"><B>THEN
    check the box for . . .</B></FONT></TD></TR>
<TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
    <TD STYLE="border-right: black 1pt solid; border-bottom: black 1pt solid; border-left: black 1pt solid; padding-top: 0.95pt; padding-left: 10.15pt; text-indent: -8.4pt"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 8pt">&#9679;&nbsp;
    Corporation</FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="border-right: black 1pt solid; border-bottom: black 1pt solid; padding-top: 0.95pt; padding-left: 3.7pt"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 8pt">Corporation</FONT></TD></TR>
<TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
    <TD STYLE="border-right: black 1pt solid; border-bottom: black 1pt solid; border-left: black 1pt solid"><P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 1.75pt; text-indent: 0in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 8pt">&#9679;&nbsp;
                                         Individual</FONT></P>
        <P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 1.75pt; text-indent: 0in"></P>
        <P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 10.15pt; text-indent: -8.4pt"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 8pt">&#9679;&nbsp;
        Sole proprietorship, or</FONT></P>
        <P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 10.15pt; text-indent: -8.4pt"></P>
        <P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 3.2pt 0pt 1.75pt; text-indent: 0in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 8pt">&#9679;&nbsp;
        Single-member limited liability company (LLC) owned by an individual and disregarded for U.S. federal tax purposes.</FONT></P></TD>
    <TD STYLE="border-right: black 1pt solid; border-bottom: black 1pt solid; padding-top: 2.25pt; padding-right: 0.65pt; padding-left: 3.7pt"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 8pt">Individual/sole
    proprietor or single- member LLC</FONT></TD></TR>
<TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
    <TD STYLE="border-right: black 1pt solid; border-bottom: black 1pt solid; border-left: black 1pt solid"><P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 10.15pt; text-indent: -8.4pt"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 8pt">&#9679;&nbsp;
                                         LLC treated as a partnership for</FONT></P>
        <P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 10.15pt; text-indent: -8.4pt"></P>
        <P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 1.7pt"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 8pt">U.S.
        federal tax purposes,</FONT></P>
        <P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 1.7pt"></P>
        <P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 3.95pt 0pt 1.75pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 8pt">&#9679;&nbsp;
        LLC that has filed Form 8832 or 2553 to be taxed as a corporation, or</FONT></P>
        <P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 3.95pt 0pt 1.75pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in"></P>
        <P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 1.3pt 0pt 1.75pt; text-indent: 0in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 8pt">&#9679;&nbsp;
        LLC that is disregarded as an entity separate from its owner but the owner is another LLC that is not disregarded for
        U.S. federal tax purposes.</FONT></P></TD>
    <TD STYLE="border-right: black 1pt solid; border-bottom: black 1pt solid; padding-top: 2.25pt; padding-right: 0.6pt; padding-left: 3.7pt"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 8pt">Limited
    liability company and enter the appropriate tax classification. (P= Partnership; C= C corporation; or S= S corporation)</FONT></TD></TR>

    <TD STYLE="border-right: black 1pt solid; border-bottom: black 1pt solid; border-left: black 1pt solid; padding-top: 0.95pt; padding-left: 10.15pt; text-indent: -8.4pt"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 8pt">&#9679;&nbsp;
    Partnership</FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="border-right: black 1pt solid; border-bottom: black 1pt solid; padding-top: 0.95pt; padding-left: 3.7pt"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 8pt">Partnership</FONT></TD></TR>

    Trust/estate</FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="border-right: black 1pt solid; border-bottom: black 1pt solid; padding-top: 0.95pt; padding-left: 3.7pt"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 8pt">Trust/estate</FONT></TD></TR>
</TABLE>
<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 6pt">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="font: bold 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 6pt">Line 4, Exemptions</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 6pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 16.4pt 0pt 6pt">If you are exempt from backup withholding and/or
FATCA reporting, enter in the appropriate space on line 4 any code(s) that may apply to you.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 16.4pt 0pt 6pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 6pt"><B>Exempt payee code.</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 6pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 8.7pt 0pt 6pt; text-indent: 0in">&#9679;<FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;
</FONT>Generally, individuals (including sole proprietors) are not exempt from backup withholding.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 8.7pt 0pt 6pt; text-indent: 0in">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 24pt 0pt 6pt; text-indent: 0in">&#9679;<FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;
</FONT>Except as provided below, corporations are exempt from backup withholding for certain payments, including interest and dividends.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 24pt 0pt 6pt; text-indent: 0in">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 8.4pt 0pt 6pt; text-indent: 0in">&#9679;<FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;
</FONT>Corporations are not exempt from backup withholding for payments made in settlement of payment card or third party network
transactions.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 8.4pt 0pt 6pt; text-indent: 0in">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 6.8pt 0pt 6pt; text-indent: 0in">&#9679;<FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;
</FONT>Corporations are not exempt from backup withholding with respect to attorneys&rsquo; fees or gross proceeds paid to attorneys,
and corporations that provide medical or health care services are not exempt with respect to payments reportable on Form 1099-MISC.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 6.8pt 0pt 6pt; text-indent: 0in">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 17.5pt 0pt 6pt; text-indent: 7pt">The following codes identify
payees that are exempt from backup withholding. Enter the appropriate code in the space in line 4.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 17.5pt 0pt 6pt; text-indent: 7pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 11.35pt 0pt 6pt; text-indent: 5pt">1&mdash;An organization exempt
from tax under section 501(a), any IRA, or a custodial account under section 403(b)(7) if the account satisfies the requirements
of section 401(f)(2)</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 11.35pt 0pt 6pt; text-indent: 5pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 24pt 0pt 11pt">2&mdash;The United States or any of its
agencies or instrumentalities</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 24pt 0pt 11pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 24pt 0pt 11pt">3&mdash;A state, the District of Columbia, a U.S. commonwealth or possession, or any of their
political subdivisions or instrumentalities</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 11pt; text-indent: -5pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 9.5pt 0pt 6pt; text-indent: 5pt">4&mdash;A foreign government or
any of its political subdivisions, agencies, or instrumentalities</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 9.5pt 0pt 6pt; text-indent: 5pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 11pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 23.3pt 0pt 6pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: 5pt">6&mdash;A
dealer in securities or commodities required to register in the United States, the District of Columbia, or a U.S. commonwealth
or possession</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 23.3pt 0pt 6pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: 5pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 6.3pt 0pt 6pt; text-indent: 5pt">7&mdash;A futures commission merchant

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 11pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 6.3pt 0pt 6pt; text-indent: 5pt">9&mdash;An entity registered at

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 6.3pt 0pt 6pt; text-indent: 5pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 6.3pt 0pt 6pt">10&mdash;A common trust fund operated by a bank
under section 584(a) 11&mdash;A financial institution</P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 6.3pt 0pt 6pt">&nbsp;</P>

as a nominee or custodian</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 5.8pt">Line 5</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 5.8pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 8.7pt 0pt 5.8pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt">Enter your address
(number, street, and apartment or suite number). This is where the requester of this Form W-9 will mail your information returns.
If this address differs from the one the requester already has on file, write NEW at the top. If a new address is provided, there
is still a chance the old address will be used until the payor changes your address in their records.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 8.7pt 0pt 5.8pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 5.8pt">Line 6</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 5.8pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 5.8pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt">Enter your city, state,
and ZIP code.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 5.8pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 5.8pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 12pt"><B>Part I. Taxpayer
Identification Number (TIN)</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 6.3pt 0pt 5.8pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><B>Enter your TIN
in the appropriate box.</B> If you are a resident alien and you do not have and are not eligible to get an SSN, your TIN is your
IRS individual taxpayer identification number (ITIN). Enter it in the social security number box. If you do not have an ITIN,
see <I>How to get a TIN</I> below.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 6.3pt 0pt 5.8pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 6.3pt 0pt 5.8pt; text-indent: 8pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt">If
you are a sole proprietor and you have an EIN, you may enter either your SSN or EIN.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 6.3pt 0pt 5.8pt; text-indent: 8pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 6.05pt 0pt 5.8pt; text-indent: 8pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt">If
you are a single-member LLC that is disregarded as an entity separate from its owner, enter the owner&rsquo;s SSN (or EIN, if
the owner has one). Do not enter the disregarded entity&rsquo;s EIN. If the LLC is classified as a corporation or partnership,
enter the entity&rsquo;s EIN.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 6.05pt 0pt 5.8pt; text-indent: 8pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 17.5pt 0pt 5.8pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><B>Note:</B> See
<I>What Name and Number To Give the Requester,</I> later, for further clarification of name and TIN combinations.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 17.5pt 0pt 5.8pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 9.95pt 0pt 5.8pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><B>How to get a
TIN.</B> If you do not have a TIN, apply for one immediately. To apply for an SSN, get Form SS-5, Application for a Social Security
Card, from your local SSA office or get this form online at <I>www.SSA.gov</I>. You may also get this form by calling 1-800-772-1213.
Use Form W-7, Application for IRS Individual Taxpayer Identification Number, to apply for an ITIN, or Form SS-4, Application for
Employer Identification Number, to apply for an EIN. You can apply for an EIN online by accessing the IRS website at <I>www.irs.gov/Businesses
</I>and clicking on Employer Identification Number (EIN) under Starting a Business. Go to <I>www.irs.gov/Forms</I> to view, download,
or print Form W-7 and/or Form SS-4. Or, you can go to <I>www.irs.gov/OrderForms</I> to place an order and have Form W-7 and/or
SS-4 mailed to you within 10 business days.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 9.95pt 0pt 5.8pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 9.95pt 0pt 5.8pt; text-indent: 8pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt">If
you are asked to complete Form W-9 but do not have a TIN, apply for a TIN and write &ldquo;Applied For&rdquo; in the space for
the TIN, sign and date the form, and give it to the requester. For interest and dividend payments, and certain payments made with
respect to readily tradable instruments, generally you will have 60 days to get a TIN and give it to the requester before you
are subject to backup withholding on payments. The 60-day rule does not apply to other types of payments. You will be subject
to backup withholding on all such payments until you provide your TIN to the requester.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 9.95pt 0pt 5.8pt; text-indent: 8pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 9.5pt 0pt 5.8pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><B>Note:</B> Entering
&ldquo;Applied For&rdquo; means that you have already applied for a TIN or that you intend to apply for one soon.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 9.5pt 0pt 5.8pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 16.85pt 0pt 5.8pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><B>Caution: </B>A
disregarded U.S. entity that has a foreign owner must use the appropriate Form W-8.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 16.85pt 0pt 5.8pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 5.8pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 12pt">Part II. Certification</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 24pt 0pt 5.8pt; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt">To
establish to the withholding agent that you are a U.S. person, or resident alien, sign Form W-9. You may be requested to sign
by the withholding agent even if item 1, 4, or 5 below indicates otherwise.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 24pt 0pt 5.8pt; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 6.3pt 0pt 5.8pt; text-indent: 8pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt">For
a joint account, only the person whose TIN is shown in Part I should sign (when required). In the case of a disregarded entity,
the person identified on line 1 must sign. Exempt payees, see <I>Exempt payee code,</I> earlier.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 6.3pt 0pt 5.8pt; text-indent: 8pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 17.5pt 0pt 5.8pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><B>Signature requirements.
</B>Complete the certification as indicated in items 1 through 5 below.</FONT></P>

</div>
<BR CLEAR="ALL"><BR>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 13.65pt 0pt 16pt; text-indent: 8pt"></P>

<!-- Field: Rule-Page --><DIV ALIGN="CENTER" STYLE="margin-top: 3pt; margin-bottom: 3pt"><DIV STYLE="font-size: 1pt; border-top: Black 1pt solid; width: 100%">&nbsp;</DIV></DIV><!-- Field: /Rule-Page -->

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 13.65pt 0pt 16pt; text-indent: 8pt">&nbsp;</P>
<DIV STYLE="POSITION:RELATIVE;FLOAT:LEFT;WIDTH:48%">
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 13.65pt 0pt 16pt; text-indent: 8pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><B>1.
Interest, dividend, and barter exchange accounts opened before 1984 and broker accounts considered active during 1983. </B>You
must give your correct TIN, but you do not have to sign the certification.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 13.65pt 0pt 16pt; text-indent: 8pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 1.65pt 0pt 16pt; text-indent: 8pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><B>2.
Interest, dividend, broker, and barter exchange accounts opened after 1983 and broker accounts considered inactive during 1983.
</B>You must sign the certification or backup withholding will apply. If you are subject to backup withholding and you are merely
providing your correct TIN to the requester, you must cross out item 2 in the certification before signing the form.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 1.65pt 0pt 16pt; text-indent: 8pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 16pt; text-indent: 8pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><B>3.
Real estate transactions.</B> You must sign the certification. You may cross out item 2 of the certification.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 16pt; text-indent: 8pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 5.8pt 0pt 16pt; text-indent: 8pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><B>4.
Other payments.</B> You must give your correct TIN, but you do not have to sign the certification unless you have been notified
that you have previously given an incorrect TIN. &ldquo;Other payments&rdquo; include payments made in the course of the requester&rsquo;s
trade or business for rents, royalties, goods (other than bills for merchandise), medical and health care services (including
payments to corporations), payments to a nonemployee for services, payments made in settlement of payment card and third party
network transactions, payments to certain fishing boat crew members and fishermen, and gross proceeds paid to attorneys (including
payments to corporations).</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 5.8pt 0pt 16pt; text-indent: 8pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0.9pt 0pt 16pt; text-indent: 8pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><B>5.
Mortgage interest paid by you, acquisition or abandonment of secured property, cancellation of debt, qualified tuition program
payments (under section 529), ABLE accounts (under section 529A), IRA, Coverdell ESA, Archer MSA or HSA contributions or distributions,
and pension distributions. </B>You must give your correct TIN, but you do not have to sign the certification.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 16pt; color: Red">&nbsp;</P>

    <TD STYLE="border-right: black 1pt solid; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; padding-top: 0.8pt; padding-left: 18.65pt; width: 50%; border-top: Black 1pt solid"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 8pt"><B>For
    this type of account:</B></FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; padding-top: 0.8pt; padding-left: 22.3pt; width: 50%; border-top: Black 1pt solid"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 8pt"><B>Give
    name and EIN of:</B></FONT></TD></TR>
<TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
    <TD STYLE="border-right: black 1pt solid; padding-top: 0.2pt; padding-right: 9.15pt; padding-left: 13.2pt; text-indent: -12pt"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 8pt">14.
    Account with the Department of Agriculture in the name of a public entity (such as a state or local government, school district,
    or prison) that receives agricultural program payments</FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="padding-top: 0.15pt; padding-left: 5.75pt"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 8pt">The
    public entity</FONT></TD></TR>
<TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
    <TD STYLE="border-right: black 1pt solid; border-bottom: black 1pt solid; padding-top: 3.2pt; padding-right: 3.8pt; padding-left: 13.25pt; text-indent: -12.05pt"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 8pt">15.
    Grantor trust filing under the Form 1041 Filing Method or the Optional Form 1099 Filing Method 2 (see Regulations section
    1.671-4(b)(2)(i)(B))</FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="border-bottom: black 1pt solid; padding-top: 3.1pt; padding-left: 5.75pt"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 8pt">The
    trust</FONT></TD></TR>
</TABLE>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 7.25pt 0pt 16pt; text-indent: -0.05pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 7.25pt 0pt 16pt; text-indent: -0.05pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SUP>1
</SUP>List first and circle the name of the person whose number you furnish. If only one person on a joint account has an SSN,
that person&rsquo;s number must be furnished.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 7.25pt 0pt 16pt; text-indent: -0.05pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 16pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SUP>2</SUP> Circle the
minor&rsquo;s name and furnish the minor&rsquo;s SSN.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 16pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 6.55pt 0pt 16pt; text-indent: -0.05pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SUP>3
</SUP>You must show your individual name and you may also enter your business or DBA name on the &ldquo;Business name/disregarded
entity&rdquo; name line. You may use either your SSN or EIN (if you have one), but the IRS encourages you to use your SSN.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 6.55pt 0pt 16pt; text-indent: -0.05pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 6.55pt 0pt 16pt; text-indent: -0.05pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><SUP>4
</SUP>List first and circle the name of the trust, estate, or pension trust. (Do not furnish the TIN of the personal representative
or trustee unless the legal entity itself is not designated in the account title.) Also see <I>Special rules for partnerships,
</I>earlier.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 6.55pt 0pt 16pt; text-indent: -0.05pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 16pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><B>*Note:</B> The grantor
also must provide a Form W-9 to trustee of trust.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 16pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 6.55pt 0pt 16pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><B>Note:</B> If
no name is circled when more than one name is listed, the number will be considered to be that of the first name listed.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 6.55pt 0pt 16pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 16pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 12pt">Secure Your Tax
Records From Identity Theft</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 9.95pt 0pt 16pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 9.95pt 0pt 16pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt">Identity theft occurs
when someone uses your personal information such as your name, SSN, or other identifying information, without your permission,
to commit fraud or other crimes. An identity thief may use your SSN to get a job or may file a tax return using your SSN to receive
a refund.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 9.95pt 0pt 16pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 24pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt">To reduce your risk:</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 24pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 16pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 6.2pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt">&#9679;</FONT></TD><TD><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt">Protect your SSN,</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 16pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 6.2pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt">&#9679;</FONT></TD><TD><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt">Ensure your employer is protecting
                                         your SSN, and</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 16pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 6.2pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt">&#9679;</FONT></TD><TD><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt">Be careful when choosing a
                                         tax preparer.</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 6.55pt 0pt 16pt; text-indent: 8pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt">If
your tax records are affected by identity theft and you receive a notice from the IRS, respond right away to the name and phone
number printed on the IRS notice or letter.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 6.55pt 0pt 16pt; text-indent: 8pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 6.55pt 0pt 16pt; text-indent: 8pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt">If
your tax records are not currently affected by identity theft but you think you are at risk due to a lost or stolen purse or wallet,
questionable credit card activity or credit report, contact the IRS Identity Theft Hotline at 1-800-908-4490 or submit Form 14039.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 6.55pt 0pt 16pt; text-indent: 8pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 9.95pt 0pt 16pt; text-indent: 8pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt">For
more information, see Pub. 5027, Identity Theft Information for Taxpayers.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 9.95pt 0pt 16pt; text-indent: 8pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 10.4pt 0pt 16pt; text-indent: 8pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt">Victims
of identity theft who are experiencing economic harm or a systemic problem, or are seeking help in resolving tax problems that
have not been resolved through normal channels, may be eligible for Taxpayer Advocate Service (TAS) assistance. You can reach
TAS by calling the TAS toll-free case intake line at 1-877-777-4778 or TTY/TDD 1-800-829-4059.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 10.4pt 0pt 16pt; text-indent: 8pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 9.95pt 0pt 16pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 8pt"><B>Protect yourself
from suspicious emails or phishing schemes. </B>Phishing is the creation and use of email and websites designed to mimic legitimate
business emails and websites. The most common act is sending an email to a user falsely claiming to be an established legitimate
enterprise in an attempt to scam the user into surrendering private information that will be used for identity theft.</FONT></P>

</div>
<BR CLEAR="ALL"><BR>

<!-- Field: Page; Sequence: 10; Value: 2 -->
    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 12pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid"><P STYLE="margin-top: 0pt; text-align: center; margin-bottom: 0pt; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><!-- Field: Sequence; Type: Arabic; Name: PageNo -->10<!-- Field: /Sequence --></P></DIV>
    <DIV STYLE="page-break-before: always; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 6pt"><P STYLE="margin: 0pt">&nbsp;</P></DIV>
    <!-- Field: /Page -->

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 6.7pt; text-indent: 8pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 6.7pt; text-indent: 8pt"></P>

<!-- Field: Rule-Page --><DIV ALIGN="CENTER" STYLE="margin-top: 3pt; margin-bottom: 3pt"><DIV STYLE="font-size: 1pt; border-top: Black 1pt solid; width: 100%">&nbsp;</DIV></DIV><!-- Field: /Rule-Page -->

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 6.7pt; text-indent: 8pt">&nbsp;</P>
<DIV STYLE="POSITION:RELATIVE;FLOAT:LEFT;WIDTH:48%">
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 6.7pt; text-indent: 8pt">The IRS does not initiate contacts
with taxpayers via emails. Also, the IRS does not request personal detailed information through email or ask taxpayers for the
PIN numbers, passwords, or similar secret access information for their credit card, bank, or other financial accounts.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 6.7pt; text-indent: 8pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 6.7pt; text-indent: 8pt">If you receive an unsolicited email
claiming to be from the IRS, forward this message to <I>phishing@irs.gov.</I> You may also report misuse of the IRS name, logo,
or other IRS property to the Treasury Inspector General for Tax Administration (TIGTA) at 1-800-366-4484. You can forward suspicious
emails to the Federal Trade Commission at <I>spam@uce.gov</I> or report them at <I>www.ftc.gov/complaint.</I> You can contact the
FTC at <I>www.ftc.gov/idtheft</I> or 877-IDTHEFT (877-438-4338). If you have been the victim of identity theft, see <I>www.IdentityTheft.gov</I>
and Pub. 5027.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 6.7pt; text-indent: 8pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 6.7pt; text-indent: 8pt">Visit <I>www.irs.gov/IdentityTheft</I>
to learn more about identity theft and how to reduce your risk.</P>

</div>
<DIV STYLE="POSITION:RELATIVE;FLOAT:RIGHT;WIDTH:48%">
<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 6.7pt"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 12pt">Privacy Act Notice</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 6.7pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 8.7pt 0pt 6.7pt">Section 6109 of the Internal Revenue Code requires
you to provide your correct TIN to persons (including federal agencies) who are required to file information returns with the IRS
to report interest, dividends, or certain other income paid to you; mortgage interest you paid; the acquisition or abandonment
of secured property; the cancellation of debt; or contributions you made to an IRA, Archer MSA, or HSA. The person collecting this
form uses the information on the form to file information returns with the IRS, reporting the above information.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 8.7pt 0pt 6.7pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 6.65pt 0pt 6.7pt">Routine uses of this information include giving
it to the Department of Justice for civil and criminal litigation and to cities, states, the District of Columbia, and U.S. commonwealths
and possessions for use in administering their laws. The information also may be disclosed to other countries under a treaty, to
federal and state agencies to enforce civil and criminal laws, or to federal law enforcement and intelligence agencies to combat
terrorism. You must provide your TIN whether or not you are required to file a tax return. Under section 3406, payers must generally
withhold a percentage of taxable interest, dividend, and certain other payments to a payee who does not give a TIN to the payer.
Certain penalties may also apply for providing false or fraudulent information.</P>

</div>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal"><A HREF="alco-sctoi_090518.htm">Alico, Inc. SC TO-I</A></FONT></P>
